         <div class="slide-content-container slide-content-center" style="display: none;">
          <div class="slide-content" style="">
           <div class="heading ">
            <div class="fusion-title-sc-wrapper fusion-block-element" style="">
             <div class="fusion-title title fusion-title-center fusion-title-size-three" style="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;">
              <div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-left">
               <div class="title-sep sep-single sep-solid" style="border-color:#FFFFFF;">
               </div>
              </div>
              <h3 class="title-heading-center" style="color:#FFFFFF;font-size:60px;line-height:80px;">
               United Way of Ventura County Thomas Fire and Flood Fund Update
              </h3>
              <div class="title-sep-container title-sep-container-right">
               <div class="title-sep sep-single sep-solid" style="border-color:#FFFFFF;">
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="caption with-bg">
            <div class="fusion-title-sc-wrapper" style="background-color: rgba(255,147,51,0.4);">
             <div class="fusion-title title fusion-sep-none fusion-title-center fusion-title-size-one" style="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;">
              <h1 class="title-heading-center" style="color:#FFFFFF;font-size:22px;line-height:26.4px;">
               Total funds raised for the United Way of Ventura County Thomas Fire and Flood fund  is $4,531,257.
 
 ·        Phase I  distribution - $375,000 in assistance.
 
 ·        Phase II distribution to date $858,972. Total for both phases – totaling $1,233,972 in Ventura County. Distribution to United Way of Santa Barbara  County - $1.1 million.
 
 ·        Phase III – Continuation of individual hardship support for those who were unaware of  the Phase II process and did not apply and to address unmet needs expressed by our agency partners for those who received support in Phase II.  Income eligibility at 120% of Area Median Income.  Assistance  to address needs of housing, livelihood and habitability of home.  Timeline June through August 31.
  
 ·        Phase IV – Long Term Recovery –   Working with the Long Term Recovery Group and their Case management  process to assist Thomas Fire affected households to plan for and achieve recovery goals. This includes assessment and verification of need, recovery plan, advocacy, and connecting clients with community support. Timeline -  September 1– December 31
              </h1>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="background background-image" data-imgwidth="1600" style="background-image: url(http://vcunitedway.org/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/Edited-flower-e1522275279170.jpg);max-width:100%;height:650px;filter: progid:DXImageTransform.Microsoft.AlphaImageLoader(src='http://vcunitedway.org/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/Edited-flower-e1522275279170.jpg', sizingMethod='scale');-ms-filter:'progid:DXImageTransform.Microsoft.AlphaImageLoader(src='http://vcunitedway.org/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/Edited-flower-e1522275279170.jpg', sizingMethod='scale')';">
         </div>
